Actor BasePointer
{
+MISSILE
+NOGRAVITY
+NOBLOCKMAP
+NOINTERACTION
-SOLID
Radius 0
Height 0
RenderStyle Add
Alpha 0.01
Scale 0.2
States
{
  Spawn:
   PNTR AAAAA 1 A_FadeIn(0.2)
   PNTR AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.06)
   Stop
}
}

Actor Pointer_Middle : BasePointer{scale 0.34}
Actor Pointer_Large : BasePointer{scale 0.60}

	Stop
   Toaster:
	TNT1 A 0
	Stop
}
}

Actor AirStrike
{
    Radius 1
    Height 60
    Speed 70
    PROJECTILE
    +CEILINGHUGGER
	+THRUActorS
    Scale 1.8
    Obituary "%o was exploded by an air strike."
	ReactionTime 255
    States
    {
    Spawn:
	    FIGT A 0
        FIGT A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("map/airstrike","Voice",0,2)
        FIGT A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AirStrikeBomb",0,random(-60,60),-5)
        FIGT A 2 A_CountDown
        Goto Spawn+2
   Death:
        FIGT A 1
        Stop
    }
}

Actor AirStrikeNoBomb : AirStrike
{
    States
    {
    Spawn:
	    FIGT A 0
        FIGT A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("map/airnobomb","Voice",0,2)
        FIGT A 2 A_CountDown
        Goto Spawn+2
   Death:
        FIGT A 1
        Stop
    }
}

Actor AirStrikeBomb
{
	Radius 8
	Height 8
	Damage 50
	Projectile
	-NOGRAVITY
	+randomIZE
	+DEHEXPLOSION
	+QUARTERGRAVITY
    +SKYEXPLODE
    +EXPLODEONWATER
	+FORCERADIUSDMG
    Scale 1.6
    Obituary "%o was exploded by an air strike."
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		BOMB A 1 Bright
		Loop
	Death:
        TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(78,684)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(256,192)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(512,128)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("OrangeParticleSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128)
	    TNT1 AA 0 A_CustomMissile("SmokeFX3",0,0,random(0,360),2,random(0,360))
        TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("Kaboom",0,0,random(0,360),2,random(0,360))
		TNT1 A 1
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("OrangeParticleSpawner",0,0,0,0, 0, 0, 0, 128)
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("Kaboom3", 0, 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("SmokeFX2", 0, 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Debris",0,0,0,random(4,-4),random(4,-4),random(4,8),0,128)
        TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(78,384)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(256,128)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(512,8)
		TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItem("RocketEx")
		Stop
	}
}

ACTOR BlueFireSpawner : T3BaseEffect
{
Scale 1.5
+DONTSPLASH
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("monster/ambientfire3")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(304) == 1, "Toaster")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlueFireEx",random(8,-8),random(4,-4),random(70,80),0,0,random(-4,-6),0,128,0)
    TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlueFire",random(18,-18),random(14,-14),random(70,80),0,0,random(-6,-8),0,128,0)
    TNT1 A 1
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR LightBlueGuruSphereSmoke : BlueGuruSmokeInheritance
{
Scale 1.8
Alpha 0.45
RenderStyle Translucent
Projectile
States
{
  Spawn:
    TNT1 A 0
    TNT1 A 1 A_Jump(256,"Spawn1","Spawn2","Spawn3")
    Stop
  Spawn1:
    TNT1 A 0 //A_SetScale(ScaleX -0.002, ScaleY -0.002)
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(Alpha<0.3,2)
    G3SM A 0 A_Explode(10,200)
    G3SM A 4 Bright A_FadeOut(0.0065)
    Loop
  Spawn2:
    TNT1 A 0 //A_SetScale(ScaleX -0.002, ScaleY -0.002)
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(Alpha<0.3,2)
    G3SM A 0 A_Explode(10,200)
    G3SM B 4 Bright A_FadeOut(0.0065)
    Loop
  Spawn3:
    TNT1 A 0 //A_SetScale(ScaleX -0.002, ScaleY -0.002)
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(Alpha<0.3,2)
    G3SM A 0 A_Explode(10,200)
    G3SM C 4 Bright A_FadeOut(0.0065)
    Loop
}
}

ACTOR TBombParticle : ClientSideEffect
{
Height 0
Radius 0
Mass 0
Damage 0
+THRUACTORS
+NOTELEPORT
+DONTSPLASH
+NOGRAVITY
+NOBLOCKMAP
+CLIENTSIDEONLY
+MISSILE
+NOBLOCKMAP
+FORCEXYBILLBOARD
+NOINTERACTION
RENDERSTYLE ADD
Alpha 0.0
BounceFactor 0.5
Scale 0.06
States
{
Spawn:
TNT1 A 0
TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(304) == 1, "Toaster")
TNT1 A 5
TNT1 A 1 A_ScaleVelocity(frandom(-0.1,-0.2))
SPKR AAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeIn(0.2)
Fly:
SPKR A 2 Bright A_FadeOut(0.06)
Loop
}
}

ACTOR RedCasing : BulletCasing
{
	Scale 0.18
	Seesound "weapons/casing1"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
	  TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(304) == 1, "Toaster")
	  CAS0 GHABCDEF 2
	  Loop
    Death:
	  TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,3)
      CAS0 A 100
      CAS0 A 5 A_FadeOut(0.10)
      Goto Death+3
      CAS0 E 100
	  CAS0 E 5 A_FadeOut(0.10)
	  Goto Death+5
	  }
}

	+NOGRAVITY
	+CLIENTSIDEONLY
	+NOINTERACTION

	States

		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(304) == 1, "Toaster")

		TNT1 A 0 A_Countdown
		Loop
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0
		Stop
	}
}

ACTOR HFCyberFireballs
{
	Game Doom
	Radius 6
	Height 8
	Speed 50
	FastSpeed 60
	Damage 35
	Projectile
	+randomIZE
	+DONTREFLECT
	+SeekerMissile
	+ExtremeDeath
	DamageType "Hell"
	RenderStyle Translucent
	Alpha 1
	Scale 2.0
    SeeSound "imp/attack"
    DeathSound "comet/explosion"
    Decal Scorch
	States
	{
	Spawn:
	TNT1 A 1
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("HFCyb/rocket", 1, 0, 2)
	Goto Fly
	Fly:
		FRTB AB 1 Bright A_SpawnItem("HFCybFireballTrail")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SeekerMissile(0,2)
		//TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile ("SuperMeteor_m_TrailFX_Smoke", 0, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (10, 40))
		Loop
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(160, 192)//Damage, Radius
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LCABaseScorch",0,0,0,0, 0, 0,random(0,359))
        TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile ("OrangeParticleSpawner", 0, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (0, 180))
		TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("CometDeathGlow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
	    EXPL A 0 Radius_Quake(15,20,0,20,0)
		TNT1 B 0 Bright A_Scream
        TNT1 A 0 A_ALertMonsters
		Goto EndAnimation
		EndAnimation:
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("SmokeFX2",random(0,10), 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("CyberSuperMeteor_m_Explosion",0,0,0,0, 0, 0, -1, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)//A_CustomMissile("Meteor_m_Explosion",0+random(5,80),0+random(35,-35),0+random(0,370))
		//TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SuperMeteor_m_FX_Smoke", 0, 0, 0, 0.01 * random(-125, 125), 0.01 * random(-125, 125), 0.01 * random(25, 245), 0, 128, 0)
		Stop
	}
}

Actor CrateDebris
{
+cannotpush
+movewithsector
+dontsplash
+noblockmap
+thruactors
+clientsideonly
+missile
Gravity 1
States
{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(304) == 1, "Toaster")
		CR4B ABCDEFGHI 4
		Goto Death
	Death:
		CR4B I 60
		CR4B I 10 A_Fadeout(0.08)
		Wait
	Toaster:
		TNT1 A 0
		Stop
	}
}

Actor CrateSplinter
{
+cannotpush
+movewithsector
+dontsplash
+noblockmap
+thruactors
+doombounce
+clientsideonly
+missile
bouncecount 3
Gravity 1
States
{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(304) == 1, "Toaster")
		TNT1 A 0 a_jump(60,"Splinter2")
		TNT1 A 0 a_jump(60,"Splinter3")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(60,"Splinter4")
		Goto Splinter1
	Splinter1:
		CR4P ABCDABCDABCDABCDABCD 2
		Goto Death
	Splinter2:
		CR4P EFEFEFEF 3
		Goto Death
	Splinter3:
		CR4P GHIJGHIJGHIJGHIJGHIJ 2
		Goto Death
	Splinter4:
		CR4P KLKLKLKLKL 3
		Goto Death
	Death:
		TNT1 A 2
		Stop
   Toaster:
		TNT1 A 0
		Stop
	}
}

ACTOR DCImpGhostA
{
Height 56
Radius 2
Alpha 0.7
RENDERSTYLE Translucent
+NONSHOOTABLE
+NOINTERACTION
+CLIENTSIDEONLY
+NONETID
States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0 Bright
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(304) == 1, "Toaster")
		TNT1 A 1 Bright
		Goto Fade
	Fade:
		DCIP A 2 A_FadeOut(0.1,1)
		Loop
	Toaster:
		TNT1 A 1 Bright
		Stop
	}
}

ACTOR PlayerResistanceParticleSpawner : RuneParticleSpawner 
{

{
  Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_ExecuteWithResult(304) == 1, "Toaster")
	TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PlayerResistanceParticle",random(16,-16),random(16,-16),random(-16,16),0,0,random(1,3),0,128,0)
	TNT1 A 1
	Stop
}
}

Actor AwakenedLegendaryRuneUpgradingCrystalSpawner : LegendaryRuneUpgradingCrystalSpawner
{
States
{
  Spawn:
	TNT1 A 5
  Death:
	TNT1 A 2
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TeleportFog",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,32)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AwakenedLegendaryRuneUpgradingCrystal",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,32)
	Stop
}
}

Actor AwakenedLegendaryRuneUpgradingCrystal : LegendaryRuneUpgradingCrystal
{
ReactionTime 65
States
{
  Spawn:	
	TNT1 A 0 
	TNT1 A 0 A_Countdown
	TRYS ABCDEDCB 4 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("TrueLegSpark",random(16,-16),random(16,-16),random(8,40),random(-6,-12),0,0,0,128,0)
	Loop
  Death:
	TNT1 A 0 
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AwakenedLegendaryRuneUpgradingCrystalLoot",0,0,16)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegendaryArchvileLightning",0,0,0)
	Stop
}
}

{

+NEVERRESPAWN
}

ACTOR AwakenedLegendaryRuneUpgradingStormBoltSpawner : LegendaryRuneUpgradingStormBoltSpawner
{

{
  Spawn:
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Wander
    TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("AwakenedLegendaryRuneUpgradingStormBolt",-18,random(0,20),random(0,360),2)
	Stop
}
}

ACTOR AwakenedLegendaryRuneUpgradingStormBolt : LegCardinalStormBolt
{
Damage 0
States
{
  Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetAngle(7 + angle)
	TNT1 A 2 A_SpawnItemEx("LegCardinalStormBoltFade",0,0,0,frandom(0.25,-0.25),frandom(0.25,-0.25),frandom(0.25,-0.25),128,0)
	Loop
  Death:
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("legstorm/explode")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlueGuruStormBoltStruckGlowX",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlueGuruStormBoltStruckGlowY",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
	TNT1 AAAAAAA 2 A_SpawnItemEx("BlueGuruSpray",random(20,-20),random(20,-20),random(30,-5),0,0,0,0,128,0)
	Stop
}
}

ACTOR AwakenedLegendaryRuneUpgradingFire : TrueSmartFire
{ 
States
{
  Spawn:
    TFIR A 2 Bright
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 12,"Death")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LVileFireSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Wander
    TFIR B 2 Bright
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LVileFireSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Wander
    TFIR C 2 Bright
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LVileFireSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Wander
    TFIR D 2 Bright
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LVileFireSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TFIR C 0 A_FireCrackle
	TNT1 A 0 A_Wander
    TFIR C 2 Bright	
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LVileFireSpawner",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Wander
    TFIR B 2 Bright
    Goto Spawn+1
  Death:
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LVileFireSpawner",0,0,0,0)
    TFIR E 2 Bright 
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LVileFireSpawner",0,0,0,0)
    TFIR F 2 Bright
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LVileFireSpawner",0,0,0,0)
    TFIR G 2 Bright 
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("LVileFireSpawner",0,0,0,0)
    TFIR H 2 Bright	
    Stop
  }
}

	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAA 17
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("legendary/strike")
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("legendary/strike","Voice",0,2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegendaryStrike")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegendaryBlueParticleSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128) 
	TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("BlueKaboom3",0,0,random(0,360),2,random(0,360))
	TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("LegendarySmokeFX2",0,0,random(0,360),2,random(0,360))
	LROC BCD 3 Bright A_SetTranslucent(0.75,1)

Actor TStrikeBeaconMarker
{
Projectile
Speed 10
WallBounceFactor 1.0
BounceFactor 1.0
RenderStyle Add
Damage 0
+BLOODLESSIMPACT
+FLOORHUGGER
+BOUNCEONACTORS
+HEXENBOUNCE
+FORCEYBILLBOARD
+SEEKERMISSILE
+SKYEXPLODE
+CANBOUNCEWATER
+THRUACTORS
Scale 1.25
Alpha 0.9
ReactionTime 525
var int user_time;
States
{
  Spawn:
	STMK A 0
  	STMK A 0 A_JumpIf(user_time >= 7,"Bomb")
	STMK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_time",user_time+1)
	STMK A 0 A_CountDown
	STMK A 0 A_RearrangePointers(AAPTR_DEFAULT,AAPTR_TRACER,AAPTR_DEFAULT)
	STMK A 2 Bright A_SeekerMissile(350,180,SMF_LOOK,256,25)
	Loop
  Bomb:
    STMK A 0
	STMK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_time",0)
	STMK A 0 A_CountDown
	STMK A 0 A_RearrangePointers(AAPTR_DEFAULT,AAPTR_TRACER,AAPTR_DEFAULT)
	STMK A 0 A_SeekerMissile(350,180,SMF_LOOK,256,25)
    SNCE A 0 A_CheckFlag(FLOAT,"SeekerBomb",AAPTR_MASTER)
	STMK A 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("TeleportedBombSpawner",0,0,0,CMF_AIMDIRECTION|CMF_TRACKOWNER)
    Goto Spawn
  SeekerBomb:
	STMK A 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("TeleportedSeekerBombSpawner",0,0,0,CMF_AIMDIRECTION|CMF_TRACKOWNER)
    Goto Spawn
  Death:
	STMK A 2 Bright A_FadeOut(0.1)
	Loop
}
}

    TNT1 A 1
    Stop
}
}

Actor LegendaryObelisk

	LGOB A 5 A_SpawnItem("LegendaryCyberFlameSpawnera",0,0,0,0)
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("Gore Nest Check Wave",0,0,0) == TRUE ,"Summoning")
	Loop
  Summoning:
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegendaryFloorLightningStrike",random(-384,384),random(-384,384))
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegendaryRuneUpgradingStormBoltSpawner",random(384,-384),random(38,-384),0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
	LGOB AAA 5 A_SpawnItem("LegendaryCyberFlameSpawnera",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegendaryFloorLightningStrike",random(-384,384),random(-384,384))
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegendaryRuneUpgradingStormBoltSpawner",random(384,-384),random(38,-384),0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
	LGOB AAA 5 A_SpawnItem("LegendaryCyberFlameSpawnera",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegendaryFloorLightningStrike",random(-384,384),random(-384,384))
	TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegendaryRuneUpgradingStormBoltSpawner",random(384,-384),random(38,-384),0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
	LGOB AAAAAAA 5 A_SpawnItem("LegendaryCyberFlameSpawnera",0,0,0,0)

    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("LegendaryObeliskOrb",0,0,96,0,0,2.0)
  Waiting:
	LGOB AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 5 A_SpawnItem("LegendaryCyberFlameSpawnera",0,0,0,0)
	LGOB AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 5 A_SpawnItem("LegendaryCyberFlameSpawnera",0,0,0,0)
	LGOB AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 5 A_SpawnItem("LegendaryCyberFlameSpawnera",0,0,0,0)
